 This Mehfil, which is decorated in a royal style, is an example of Banarasi irrationality
 jahaan har kisi ke upar gulabon kii pankhudiyon kii bauchhaar hoti he, to gulab jal kii phuhaar logon ko gudgudati bhi he
 This environment also makes the mood of the weather change colorful
 padmabhushan chhannu laal kehete hai, "yah banaras kii bahut puraani parampara he
 When the weather changes, such an event between teal roses and music gives a feeling of that archaic tradition of Banaras, in which our culture is well established and it gives us a lot of coolness
 is gulabi mehafil main shirkat karne waalon kaa gulab kii pankhudiyo or paan kii gilori se swaagat kiya jaataa he
 On which the famous coolness of Banaras compliments his mood
 halki gulabi thand ke bich jab tanpure se madhur shastreey sangeet kaa swar nikalataa he, to aisa lagata he maano khule aasmaan tale neelambar main saji is mehfil kii gulabi taan se prakruti bhi jhum rahi he
 Initially Gulab Bari was organized in the court of King Maharaja
 itihaas ke is lambey safar main is parampara ne kai utaar-chadhaav bhi dekhe, lekin iske kadradaanon kii kami kabhi bhi nahin rahi
 This Gulabbadi of Banaras has also started becoming an example of communal harmony
 badi bazaar ke nivasee samim ansaari pichley kai saalon se yahaan logon ko thandai pilaane kaa jimmaa sambhalate hai
 Ansari fearlessly explains that the wait for Gulabbadi is no less than Eid
 hindu, musalmaan, sikh, isai ke alaava ise dekhne ke liye saat samandar paar se bhi log yahaan chale aate hai or har koi masti ke rang main dub janaa chahta he
 Perhaps this is the reason that Gulab Bari is now becoming an identity of Benaras along with fun

 ) The president of the World Medical Association (WMA), the apex body of doctors around the world, has on Friday appointed an Indian doctor who has allegations of corruption, and his appointment is being debated as legal cases are pending against him
 
 dablyueme dwaara jari kiye gaye bayaan main kaha gaya he ki dow kethan desai ne shuukravaar ko association ke adhyaksh ke rup main taiwan main hui uski vaarshik baithak ke dauraan udghaatan bhaashan diya
 He will remain the president of the association for 2016 / 17
 varsh 2009 main dablyueme ke bhavi adhyaksh chune jane ke vakt se dow kethan desai ke khilaaf shadyantr rachane tathaa bhrashtachar ke aarope lagate rahe hai
 Dr
 Ketan Desai has denied any wrongdoing in the context of pending cases
 unhone un sawaalon ke jawaab nahin die, jo roitre ne unhen email ke zariye bheje the
 When Reuters asked the WMA this week about updates on the legal status of Dr
 Ketan Desai, WMA spokesman Nigel Duncan said the association had nothing to say about it
 dancan ne kaha, "mujhe nahin lagata, jo ham pehle kah chuke hai, uske alaava hamen kuch or kahana he
 
 
 "he also did not respond to legal cases issued against Dr
 Ketan Desai, nor did he reply to what he has been told about these cases in recent months
 nai dilli main varsh 2010 main darj hue ek maamle main dow kethan desai par ek medical college se do karod rupee kii rishwat lene kii saazish main kathith rup se shaamil hone ko lekar bhrashtachar tathaa aapraadhik shadyantr rachane ke aarope lagaae gaye hai
 Investigators alleged that Dr
 Desai helped the medical college to get permission from the Medical Council to enroll more students
 pichley saal jab college (jo is maamle main prativaadee nahin he) se sampark kiya gaya, unhone tippanee karne se inkaar kar diya
 Dr
 Desai was sent to prison that same year, and his appearance as WMA president was suspended
 unhen baad main zamaanat par reeha kiya gaya
 In 2013, the WMA also lifted the suspension of Dr Desai's claim to the post of president after receiving assurances from the Indian Medical Association (IMA)
 dow desai ieme ke adhyaksh bhi rah chuke hai
 The IMA has also not responded to queries sent by Reuters this week
 roitre dwaara kii gai or pichley saal july main prakashit kii gai jaanch se pataa chalata he ki ieme ne galat tareeke se dablyueme ko bataaya tha ki dow desai ke khilaaf lage aarope waapas le liye gaye hai
 This information was accepted by the big doctor organizations as true
 pichley saal ieme ne kaha tha ki unhone dablyueme ko kabhi gumraah nahin kiya
 The WMA said that they took the questions raised in an article published by Reuters 'very seriously' and would be investigated
 baad main, oktober, 2015 main dablyueme ne bina koi kaaran bataae dow desai ko adhyaksh banane kaa apana faisla barkaraar rakh liya
 a CBI source said this week that the case in New Delhi is still going on, though it is pending due to pendency of appeals made in the Supreme Court
 sutara ne bataaya ki dow desai ko jila jaj kii adaalat main sunwaayee ke dauraan haazir hona padataa he
 The comments 3 agast kaa ek court dastauez bataata he ki urologist dow desai ne us taarikh par court se gaiyrhaazir hone kii anumati beemaari ke aadhaar par maangi thi
 The next hearing in the case is to be held on November 4
 © Thomson Reuters 2016 The statement issued by the WMA stated that Dr
 Ketan Desai gave the inaugural address on Friday during its annual meeting in Taiwan as the president of the association
 vah 2016 / 17 ke liye association ke adhyaksh rahenge
 Ever since he was elected the future president of the WMA in 2009, there have been allegations of conspiracy and corruption against Dr
 Ketan Desai
 lambit maamalon ke sandarbh main dow kethan desai ne koi bhi galat kaam kiya hone se inkaar kiya he
 He did not answer questions Reuters had sent to him via email
 jab roitre ne isi saptaah dablyueme se dow kethan desai kii kanoonee sthiti par apadet ke bare main poocha, dablyueme pravaktaa nigel dancan ne kaha ki association ko is bare main kuch or nahin kahana he
 "I don't think we have anything to say other than what we've said before," Duncan said
 
 
 " unhone dow kethan desai ke khilaaf jari kanoonee keson par bhi koi jawaab nahin diya, or na hi is baat ko uttar diya ki haalia maheenon main unhen in keson ke bare main kya bataaya gaya he
 In a case registered in New Delhi in the year 2010, Dr
 Ketan Desai has been accused of corruption and criminal conspiracy for his alleged involvement in the conspiracy to take a bribe of Rs 2 crore from a medical college
 jaanchakartaaon ne aarope lagaaya ki dow desai ne medical council se adhik chaatro ko daakhila dene kii anumati hasil karne main medical college kii madad kii
 Last year when the college (which is not the defendant in the case) was contacted, he declined to comment
 dow desai ko usee saal jail bhej diya gaya tha, or dablyueme adhyaksh ke rup main unka pesh kiya janaa nilambit kar diya gaya
 He was later released on bail
 varsh 2013 main dablyueme ne bhi indian medical association (ieme) kii taraf se aashwaasan milane ke baad dow desai kii adhyaksh pad par daavedaari par lage nilamban ko hataa diya
 Dr
 Desai has also been the President of IMA
 isi saptaah roitre dwaara bheje gaye sawaalon kaa ieme ne bhi koi jawaab nahin diya he
 The investigation, conducted by Reuters and published in July last year, shows that the IMA wrongly told the WMA that the charges against Dr
 Desai had been withdrawn
 is jaankaree ko bade doctor sanghathanon ne sach maanakar sweekaar kar liya
 Last year, the IMA said they never misled the WMA
 dablyueme ne kaha tha ki unhone roitre dwaara prakashit lekh main uthaae gaye sawaalon ko 'bahut gambhirtha' se liya tha, or unki jaanch karai jaaegi
 Later, in October 2015, the WMA upheld its decision to make Dr
 Desai the chairman without assigning any reason
 sibiai ke ek sutara ne isi saptaah bataaya ki nai dilli vaala maamla ab bhi jari he, haalanki vah supreme court main kii gai apil ke pending hone kii vajah se lambit he
 The source said that Dr
 Desai has to appear in the district judge's court during the hearing
 tippaniyan a 3 August court document states that the urologist Dr Desai had sought permission from the court to appear on that date on the basis of illness
 maamle main agali sunwaayee 4 november ko honi he

 Google Email advises all email services to use special characters and any number in their password
 haalanki adhiktar log ise gambhirtha se nahin lete hai
 But many times the ID gets hacked even though the password is strong
 aisa aapke saath na ho isliye yahaan bataae gaye tips ko dhyaan main rakhen
 Follow these tips even if you have added special characters and numbers to the password
 recovery detailemail account main apana sahi mobile number or duusari email idi darj karke rakhen, jiskaa aap istemaal kar rahe hai
 Both of these will help you in recovery of account hack
 iske alaava security ansar aisa den jo aapako yaad rahe
 Secure password: Keep an upper case, a lower case, a special character and a numeric in your password
 aisa nahin karenge to havers bahut aasaani se aapke email idi main send laga lenge
 Two Step Authentication Almost all major email services including Gmail offer the option of two step authentication
 chahen to ise inable kar len
 For this, go to Security Settings and enter your mobile number
 isse har baar log-in karne ke liye aapke mobile par veriphication kii bheji jaaegi jiske jariye email log-in hoga

 Hackers send malware through attachments
 aap jaise hi atachament kholte hai aapke computers main kuch mailaware thikaana bana lete hai
 Then slowly they read your behavior and send your log-in details to their boss or hackers
